name:D‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äç ‚ÄçP‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äç ‚ÄçH‚Äça‚Äço
info:1 King Bed Standard
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted March 2, 2024
msg:This is a rare hotel with excellent software and hardware

I checked in on 2/28 and was lucky enough to be upgraded to a room type. Since it was raining that day, I casually asked where I could go shopping nearby. The receptionist at the counter explained clearly and carefully what attractions there were nearby, and even The most suitable time period for each nearby attraction is informed one by one. I have stayed in hundreds of five-star hotels, and such careful and considerate introductions are indeed extremely rare, and it is really great.

The quality of the room is very good, and there is no sense of inconsistency between Chinese and Western styles. Whether you like tea or coffee, you can find everything you need, the bed and pillows are of moderate hardness, there are double sinks and an impeccable full-function disposable toilet. In short, every setting in the room is perfect. All are just right to make people feel comfortable.

The package I stayed in included breakfast and dinner. The dinner was on the second floor. I didn‚Äôt expect much at first, but after each dish was served one by one, it was completely worthy of a five-star level. There was no compromise at all because it was a complimentary dinner. There were very few people in the restaurant that day. If you come to stay, it is recommended that you choose this itinerary that includes dinner.

Breakfast is a type with many styles but good texture. However, there are two dishes that I feel are not very up to standard. For example, one dish feels that the peas in it are too old. However, only one or two of the dozen dishes are not good. Among them, I especially like tofu. As for the brain, the fruit is also great, not the kind of bland fruit. In short, regardless of breakfast or dinner, I can give it a rating of 85-90 points.

The location of this hotel is excellent. It is within walking distance of many attractions. I have lived in Shanghai for ten years. I have always felt that the most beautiful thing in Shanghai is not the Bund, but the old and new areas of Hengshan Road, Hunan Road and Wukang Road. neighborhood, then walk instead of taking a taxi or driving to the scenic spots to enjoy the sights, so that you can slowly experience the Shanghai style.

The last thing I want to say is that when I go to Shanghai in the future, this hotel will definitely be on my first choice list. It is too difficult to find a hotel with such good service, good location and excellent hardware.

It is positioned as a boutique resort hotel and a business hotel. Basement parking is very convenient, which is far more than other downtown hotels. The first floor of the hotel surrounds the inner courtyard, and the rest area is arranged around the courtyard. A large number of artworks enhance the artistic and cultural a**osphere of the hotel. Although the hotel is not big, it still does a good job of separating the public area and the guest room area. The swimming pool in the public area and the cafeteria with terrace are the highlights of the hotel. In terms of decoration quality, although it is not newly decorated, it is well maintained and very comfortable.

msg:I saw a lot of bad reviews on the Internet before booking. I was a bit uneasy, but I actually felt pretty good after staying for a few days. Very good hotel.

The first advantage is that the location is very good, directly above Hengshan Road subway, opposite Yonganli, walk to Xuhui. The design of the whole building is also good. The balcony of the garden-view room faces the atrium, making it quiet during the day and night. Huang Mei Tianwo is very comfortable drinking coffee on the balcony. The hotel has upgraded the deluxe room, which is said to be bigger than the superior room. Anyway, the space for one person is very large. I feel that a couple with a child may be enough. The other thing is that the service is very good. From check-in to check-out, the staff I met were very professional and courteous. The cleaning aunt would greet me in the corridor every day. Did not encounter the cold-faced situation mentioned on the Internet.

Finally, the facilities are good. Because I lived for several days, the gym pool was used all over the place. The equipment is perfect and clean. The best thing is that there is a dryer in the dressing room, so you don‚Äôt need to bring your wet swimsuit back to the room after swimming. There is also a steam room upstairs in the dressing room. The facilities are relatively old, but there are not many people, and it is good to use.

The disadvantage is that the room facilities are relatively old, and cleaning needs to be strengthened. It can be seen that the hotel was originally built as a five-star hotel, but after several licensing changes, the room facilities really need to be updated. There are quite a few marks on the carpet and sofa. A piece of hair was found on the sofa on the night of the stay, but the overall hygiene score was over 85.

Generally speaking, the price/performance ratio is relatively high. If you come to Shanghai frequently, this one can join one of the permanent hotels.
